class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本期绪论：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1/2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月遭抓捕、已被羁押了<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月的湖南</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">人权捍卫者、南方街头运动践行者谢文飞（本名谢丰夏）于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被中共当局判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，随后被转监到湖南赤山监狱。其在关押期间遭受酷刑，身体状况堪忧。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">“广州<span lang="EN-US">11</span>·<span lang="EN-US">12</span>大抓捕”案已经宣判，资深民运人士范一平获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，胡天峰获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，另范文成等人刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西人权律师常玮平于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被宝鸡市凤县法院一审以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。目前被羁押于宝鸡市凤县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">中国拆墙运动（<span lang="EN-US">BanGFW</span>）发起人、拆墙宝典”写作和推动者、海外民主派人士，乔鑫鑫（本名杨泽伟）在六四<span lang="EN-US">34</span>周年纪念日前夕的<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，突遭中国警方跨境抓捕；后知其在当地侨领、老挝警方的连手配合下被中国警方野蛮绑架，自此失联，至今下落不明。目前被羁押地点缺详。乔鑫鑫（本名杨泽伟）：<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，湖南省祁东县人，客居老挝的中国公民，新闻媒体人，前广州市某新闻媒体职员，前自由亚洲电台驻东南亚特约记者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5/</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">中共当局对法轮功的残酷镇压仍然是持续不断，但法轮功学员的反抗也依然是一如既往，毫不畏惧。本期又收集了<span lang="EN-US">40</span>位被判刑的法轮功学员的名单和简历。这是每个月遭到中共判刑的数量最大的群体。<span lang="EN-US"> <o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">以上内容均记录于在本报告的各个相关部分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">以下是本期报告的全部内容。</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">前言：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集和编撰，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">93</span></b>期。至此，本报告发布历时已整整七年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历仍可见移除时的当期附录。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年多来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">七年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">以此</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">七年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">本网邮箱：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="mailto:wqw2011@gmail.com"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 0; mso-list: l12 level1 lfo21; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">48</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千字</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">，分八部分发布。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。上期名单中</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">33</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人已被</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放或取保获释。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留的<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">6</span>人</b>以及被判刑的<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">43</span></b>人，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">合计<span lang="EN-US">49</span>人的</b>名单及简介。目前，本期报告录入发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1579</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。报告将以此顺序标准刊发每一位在押政治犯、良心犯的简介。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk507373588"></a><a name="_Hlk507373498"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">二、本月获悉上期名录中被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人的名单<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></a></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><b minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: 11.0pt;">本期在押已判的政治犯、良心犯名单是按照被判刑期的年限长短顺序——即由死刑正在核准、死缓、无期徒刑至有期徒刑、刑期不详及羁押未判，来进行统计的。名单如下：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><span class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">A.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿布杜热扎克•夏木西丁（维吾尔）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿布拉江·阿乌提·阿有普（<span lang="EN-US">Ablajan Awut Ayup</span>）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿尔恒•巴杂尔别克（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿斯哈·阿孜提别克（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿提开姆•茹孜</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿旺益西（藏）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、阿吾勒别克·努尔加合蒲（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿亚桑扎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">艾朝玉、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">艾尔肯•吐尔逊（维）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、艾济孜•阿卜杜拉、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">艾山江•卡日（维）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">艾则孜•艾买提（维）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安然、昂扎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">奥坎（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">阿布都热扎克·沙依木</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">1957</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月出生，新疆维吾尔自治区阿克苏地区柯坪县人，维吾尔族名：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;;">‎</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">Abdurazaq Sayim </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;">ئابدۇرازاق</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;"> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt;">سايىم</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">，新疆乌鲁木齐市新城区北京路街道中英公小区居民，中共党员，公职人员，早期曾为新疆自治区教育厅工农教育处、自治区成人招生办和自治区招生办干事，后任自治区招生办副主任、新疆教育报刊社副总编、阿克苏地区温宿县委副书记、自治区教委勤工俭学办主任，原新疆教育出版社党委副书记、社长、副总编，原新疆社会科学院党委委员、副院长，以沙塔尔·沙吾提为首的分裂国家犯罪集团的要犯之一，中共新疆当局指称的“双面人”，中国在押政治犯。自</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年以来，因中共新疆当局对维吾尔族等各少数族裔实行更严格的高压管控，其虽长期就职于当局任命的高级公职岗位上，但依然为中共新疆当局视为可猜疑得异己，暗中监控，收集欲打压资料；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">29</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日，其被新疆维吾尔自治区纪委突然以涉嫌严重违纪为由停职工作，接受组织调查；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">25</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日，经新疆自治区党委批准，准予自治区纪委对其严重违纪问题进行立案审查；后其被很快开除党籍、开除公职（即“双开”）和收缴违纪所得，且自治区纪委将其涉嫌犯罪问题及线索移送至新疆维吾尔自治区检察院处置；同年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日，其案被自治区检察院以涉嫌“受贿罪”立案侦查，并采取强制措施，指控其因十数年“严重违反政治纪律；严重违反廉洁纪律，收受礼金”和“严重违反国家法律法规，利用职权或者地位形成的便利条件，通过直接安排或向他人打招呼的方式，在企业经营、承揽工程等方面为他人谋取利益，索要、收受巨额财物”，故而涉嫌犯罪，应予批捕；后被又追加罪责，认定其为“以沙塔尔·沙吾提为首的分裂国家犯罪集团”的要犯之一，提起公诉；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月，其一行多人案在新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市法院开庭审理，最终其被以“受贿罪”、“分裂国家政权罪”等多项罪名判处无期徒刑；其等不服判决，立即上诉，最高法院已驳回上诉，维持原判；截至目前，一直无法获取其具体信息。目前服刑地址不明。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">阿布杜热扎克•夏木西丁（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊宁市人，伊宁市克拜克玉孜村农民，曾当过木工，维吾尔名<span lang="EN-US">Abdurazzak Shamseden</span>，新疆著名持不同政见者。<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年曾因其胞弟萨迪尔丁·夏木西丁<span lang="EN-US">(Sadirdin Shamseden)</span>发起一个旨在解决维吾尔人酗酒及毒品泛滥等社会问题的民间草根运动（又叫“麦西莱普活动”），其亦参与其中。尽管几年间该运动发展日益壮大，覆盖了几乎整个伊宁周边地区，但终因碰触到中共高层的敏感神经，引起中共新疆当局的极度恐慌，遂遭强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年麦西莱普活动被政府明令禁止；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日新疆伊宁发生维吾尔族市民大规模抗议游行示威，虽被很快强力镇压，但之后伊宁地区的胡迪亚玉孜村又发生了警民冲突，且又有六人被军警枪杀，因其外甥哈穆提•莫哈买提<span lang="EN-US">(Hemmat Muhemmet)</span>是警民冲突中死亡青年之一，所以其亦被怀疑参与其中。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被当局抓捕，并被指控与<span lang="EN-US">2.5</span>伊宁抗议示威及本次警民冲突有关；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月其被伊宁市中级法院以“分裂国家罪”判处无期徒刑，剥夺政治权利终身；其不服上诉，二审后依然维持原判；据悉其惨遭刑讯逼供和极端非人待遇；审讯和审判期间，几乎所有人道权利及法律基本权利均被剥夺，既无任何法律代理，又不准与家属见面，其家属不仅没有接到审判日通知，判决书中也无确切审判日期，亲属只是在上诉截止日前三天，才由小道消息获此判决信息。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐第一监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿布拉江·阿乌提·阿有普（<span lang="EN-US">Ablajan Awut Ayup</span>）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区和田地区皮山县人，著名维吾尔族新生代歌手，艺名“<span lang="EN-US">AJ</span>”，艺术家，<span lang="EN-US">Nice</span>品牌新疆代言人，维吾尔文化倡导者、推广者，中国在押政治犯。近年来，因逐渐成为集作词、作曲、编曲、演唱、舞蹈于一身的全能实力派偶像歌手，可演唱国语、英语和维吾尔等多种语言歌曲，故而深受维吾尔人喜爱；因其所在区域以穆斯林居民为主体，深感少数族裔正在被中共当局逐步歧视、弱化和边缘化，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日接受英国<span lang="EN-US">BBC</span>新闻网记者采访，公开表达希望通过其音乐联结汉维两族之间的文化，不料却触碰了中共对新疆少数族裔意识形态在政治上严控的敏感神经，随后遭到中共新疆当局无情打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，被和田地区警方莫名带走，关进再教育集中营，数月后又被以不具名罪由转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其被新疆和田市地方法院已秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，罪名不详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月；据悉，其被重判与赞美、推动维吾尔文化及接受过英国<span lang="EN-US">BBC</span>新闻网采访有关。目前服刑监狱不详。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/11.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/11.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿尔恒•巴杂尔别克（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿斯哈·阿孜提别克（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族，原伊宁市飞机场路<span lang="EN-US">61</span>号北苑别墅区居民，前伊犁哈萨克自治州察布查尔锡伯自治县粮食局官员，原伊犁哈萨克自治州政府移民管理局退休干部，哈萨克国籍公民，中国在押政治犯。因其曾在伊犁州政府移民管理局工作期间，接触过伊犁河流域水利工程的移民搬迁工作，熟知伊犁河是中哈国际河流和涉伊犁河流域相关水利工程项目，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月又与哈萨克共和国驻中国乌鲁木齐签证代办处副主任达尼亚尔·赛力克巴耶夫<span lang="EN-US">(SERIKBAYEV DANIYAR)</span>相结识，遂遭中共新疆当局的高度警觉、监控与强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，其已移民至哈萨克斯坦国（以下简称“哈国”），并于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月加入哈国国籍；但<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其被强行驾车驶入中国霍尔果斯口岸至哈国国际市场路段的哈国境内自由贸易区的中国新疆警方跨境绑架，自此失联；尽管其已移民并加入哈国国籍，但仍被中共政府视为新疆居民，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被伊犁哈萨克自治州霍城县警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被霍城县警方以同罪由转正式逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其案被霍城县检察院以“间谍罪”和“诈骗罪”起诉至新疆维吾尔自治区高级法院伊犁哈萨克自治州分院，指控其曾在伊犁州政府移民管理局任职期间，结识了哈国民族安全委员会成员，并按其要求对伊犁河流域水利设施及河流进行拍照，提供水利设施信息等，该行为触犯了中国法律，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被该法院秘密审判，以“间谍罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，以“诈骗罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，数罪并罚，最后执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前被羁押于伊犁哈萨克自治州霍城县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿提开姆•茹孜：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1991</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Atikem Rozi</span>，又译为阿提克木·如孜，维吾尔著名学者伊力哈木•土赫提的学生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>“维吾尔在线”网站前义工，维吾尔人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2010</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年—<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，曾因个人护照申请连续三次被当局以政治原因而拒发（尽管其无任何政治不良记录），故而将其遭遇发布于新浪微博之上，随后各大媒体，如官方刊物《都市北京》<span lang="EN-US">(Metro Beijing)</span>、“维吾尔在线”和中国《环球时报》等媒体便竞相刊发或转载了涉及其本人与其他维吾尔人申请护照时遭遇双重标准的文章，引发社会热议；此一事件因很快触动了中共当局的敏感神经，遂遭到中共新疆当局的严厉打击和报复；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被乌鲁木齐警方以在“媒体上辩论”为由传唤，且被审问<span lang="EN-US">6</span>小时后才得以获释，两天之后又到其家继续威吓、骚扰；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因其多次使用<span lang="EN-US">twitter,facebook</span>以及新浪微博等网站发布文章和讯息，并利用网媒广泛寻找被失踪多日的男友、维吾尔人权捍卫者穆塔力普•伊明，随被以背景是维吾尔著名学者伊力哈木•土赫提在北京的学生、曾是“维吾尔在线”网站义工为罪由被北京市警方传唤，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日其等<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人被以涉嫌“分裂国家罪”统一刑拘（但据官方报道，其于<span lang="EN-US">2014 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">1 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被拘留）；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其案被定为“分裂国家犯罪集团案”，故被新疆乌鲁木齐市检察院正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后，其一行<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人案在乌鲁木齐巿中级法院一起开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人终被乌鲁木齐巿中级法院统一宣判<span lang="EN-US">3-8</span>年不等刑期；其中，其被以“分裂主义罪”和“危害国家安全罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，理应刑满释放，但据中国环球电视网（又称中国国际电视台，英文简称<span lang="EN-US">CGTN</span>）在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月发布的一部宣传片中显示，其身着囚服出现在镜头前，故其是否如期释放，或是否被释放后又重新拘留，不得而知。目前或仍在新疆女子监狱（又名新疆第二监狱，新疆乌鲁木齐市新市区东站路<span lang="EN-US">1327</span>号女子监狱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">830013</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_5.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_5.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿旺益西：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，藏族名<span lang="EN-US">NgawangYeshe</span>，西藏自治区日喀则市人，日喀则市定日县协格尔镇查那村当卓寺（藏民称之为（<span lang="EN-US">Tengdro</span>））僧侣，公益慈善捐助人，藏族异见人士，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>月，因当卓寺僧人曲嘉旺波（<span lang="EN-US">Choegyal Wangpo</span>）到西藏首府拉萨市做佛事访问时不甚将手机遗失在某咖啡馆，后被老板交予拉萨市警方处置；但因警方在查阅手机时，发现内存其及当卓寺众僧侣与尼泊尔同乡藏僧的聊天记录，尤其是存有<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月尼泊尔大地震时，他们向那里的藏民和寺院捐款赈灾等的信息记录，以及还存有和第<span lang="EN-US">14</span>世达赖喇嘛有关的照片及相关文献等；遂立即触碰到中共西藏当局的政治敏感神经，认定这是一起与境外敌对势力勾结，利用网络通讯对国家安全构成威胁的典型案件；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其所在当卓寺突遭日喀则市当局派出的大批武警及公安警察袭击，所有僧人均被强迫接受政治洗脑教育数天，多人遭殴打；之后有<span lang="EN-US">20</span>名僧侣（含其在内）被刑拘，当卓寺及其附近的网络被切断；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天后，除一名僧侣因向当局抗议而自杀，其余<span lang="EN-US">19</span>名僧人仍被羁押，数月不放；后其与曲嘉旺波等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名藏僧均被日喀则市检察院以涉嫌“跟境外藏人联系、赈济尼泊尔地震，或拥有和达赖喇嘛有关照片或文献”为罪由予以批捕，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日获悉，其已被西藏自治区日喀则市中级法院以“危害国家安全罪”枉法判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月；其余三名僧侣亦被以同罪名分别重判<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-17</span>年不等。目前疑似在拉萨市札基监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿吾勒别克·努尔加合蒲（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US">Ayelbek Nurzhahp</span>，伊犁州昭苏县阿克达拉镇清真寺伊玛目（即宗教仪式领祷人或主持），中国在押良心犯。早年曾就读于伊犁特克斯县宗教学校，毕业后被官方指定为昭苏县清真寺的伊玛目（即宗教仪式领祷人或主持），管辖服务于当地<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个清真寺；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾多次到哈萨克共和国（简称哈国）访问；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因感觉新疆政治气氛欠佳而将妻子和两个孩子送到哈国，其本人亦打算将自己在新疆的不动产（包括牲畜等）变卖后移民哈国，不料被中共新疆当局知晓，遂被警方以“不准移民哈国”为由抓捕，并遭威胁让其全家（含其妻子和孩子）务必返回国内生活；其全家虽按要求照办，但<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日仍被昭苏县警方突然抓走，并被关押在当地的政治再教育营；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被昭苏县警方以“全家要移民哈国”为罪由正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，知其被伊犁哈萨克自治州昭苏县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年，罪名不详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2042</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日；据悉，在被判决时，法院竟称让其“自己选择罪名，然后给判刑”；其妻、其弟被送政治再教育营教育，后亦被以同罪由各判<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年。目前在生产建设兵团农七师高泉监狱（新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">833200</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿亚桑扎（藏族）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">青海省果洛州牧民。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿亚桑扎是因为上访被抓捕的，<span lang="EN-US"> 2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，因为他经牧民选举当上牧委会主任，却被官方把<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年已经了结的案件，重新拿出来说事把他抓捕冤屈判刑一年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，上诉也被维持原判。阿亚桑扎<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午在果洛州高速路口上访途中，被公安人员抓捕连夜送到西宁次日送到了乐都区看守所。阿亚桑扎对自己被关押到离果洛州<span lang="EN-US">600</span>公里外的看守所感到不可理解，认为这是官方对他的一种折磨。他被抓时正在带领大家控告相关人员贪污犯罪的事情进展情况，要大家继续坚持控告下去。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，阿亚桑扎被当局判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑。阿亚桑扎等所谓涉恶案件开庭两天当庭宣判，其对获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年当庭表示不服提起上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">艾朝玉<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成都市法轮功学员。刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被成都公安局成华分局国保、双水碾派出所警察抄家并抓捕。刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被成华区公安分局批捕，关押在郫县看守所。构陷他们的所谓「案件」曾两次退回侦查机关。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，成华区检察院把刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇起诉到成华区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇，在成都市成华区法院一楼视频开庭，分别被判刑八年。庭审结束后，夫妻俩与家人坚决不服判决，马上要求上诉，并请律师继续代理二审。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/8.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">艾尔肯·吐尔逊（维）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁州人，伊犁自治州伊宁市墩买里街道墩买里小区公民，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Erkin Tursun</span>，曾为中学历史老师，后为新闻媒体人，“伊犁儿童培训中心”（学校）创办人和负责人，伊犁广播电视台记者、编辑和导演，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年度伊犁新闻界十大人物之一，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代初期，曾就读于新疆大学历史系，并取得本科学位；大学毕业后，曾在一中学担任历史老师，并为该校学生组织过多项课余活动；同期，曾组建过一个名为“<span lang="EN-US"> Arzu</span>”（“希望”）的艺术团，因该团由歌手、喜剧演员、舞蹈演员和演员组成，并将在新疆各地进行公开表演，遂颇受公众欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代中期，开始到伊犁广播电视台工作，并开设和经营了一所名为“伊犁儿童培训中心”（<span lang="EN-US">yash-osmurlerniterbiyelesh merkizi</span>）的学校，旨在提供舞蹈课后指导和唱歌、拳击、语言、科学及新闻学等课程的培训（后拳击课被政府取消）；后因该培训中心效果斐然，曾获得许多国家甚至国际表现奖，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年被并入地区政府儿童培训中心，并仍由其担任维吾尔族负责人；又因其在伊犁广播电视台做记者期间，制作了多起节目，并多次荣获不同地区与国家项目奖，而且，还制作、执导过多部电影、儿童歌曲、音乐剧和纪录片（如“<span lang="EN-US"> Chin Tomur Batur</span>”、“<span lang="EN-US"> Sirlik Ongkur</span>”、“<span lang="EN-US"> Rehimsiz Chush</span>”和“<span lang="EN-US"> Tutunge AylanghanMuhebbet</span>” 等），反响甚好，故而深得伊宁市政府赞许；曾因在电视台担任儿童电视节目《希望的眼睛》主持人和导演（被捕前后该节目仍在播出中），而颇受儿童观众及其家长的欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾荣获该年度伊利新闻界十大人物之一，并将当地古尔哈市（译音）一家购物中心以其名（<span lang="EN-US">Erkin</span>）命名；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，其突然被伊宁市警方以涉嫌“恐怖主义”、“煽动民族仇恨”和帮助“罪犯”为罪由拘捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被伊宁市中级法院以“危害罪犯和煽动民族仇恨或歧视罪” 和“包庇罪”等多项罪名重判有期徒刑判刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。目前在新疆新源监狱（新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁州新源县喀拉布拉镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">835813</span>）服刑。信<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/1910.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/1910.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">艾济孜·阿卜杜拉<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">维吾尔族，新疆维巴音郭楞蒙古自治州（简称巴音郭楞州、巴州）库尔勒市人，库尔勒市铁克其乡阿依丁阔力村（<span lang="EN-US">Aydinkol</span>）公民，职业农民，穆斯林，中国在押良心犯。因笃信伊斯兰教，遂经常与家人、亲友及所在村庄的穆斯林村民私下里诵读《古兰经》、做信仰祷告和参与信仰仪式；但是，近些年来，尤其是自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年以来，中共政府针对新疆地区各少数族裔（尤以维吾尔族、哈萨克族、回族等为甚）的高压管控达到空前地步，大批的维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族等民众被尽可能多地强制性送进（实为关押）再教育培训基地（俗称“再教育营”）进行洗脑式判刑，故而其及家人，以及多名亲朋好友等尽被严打监控；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-3</span>月，其与其两个儿子、五个女儿、儿媳和村中<span lang="EN-US">20%</span>的其他村民均被库尔勒市铁克其乡警方抓走，送再教育营进行洗脑式教育培训；很快，其又被库尔勒市警方以在田间浇灌庄稼时进行了“非法宗教活动”和“非法集会”为罪由转为刑拘；后又被库尔德市检察院以同罪由予以批捕，指控其因将非法宗教活动和非法集会又带到“再教育营”中，使有害信息不断蔓延，遂其言行与国家有关新疆管控规定或条例相抵触，应予以批捕和判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，其案在新疆维吾尔自治区巴音郭楞州库尔勒市法院开庭受审，后被一审以“非法宗教活动罪”和“非法集会罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月；据悉，其两个儿子虽未被判刑，但释放回家仅过了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>周，就又都被库尔勒市警方带走，并被分别送往新疆巴音郭楞州若羌县罗布泊镇和新疆喀什地区喀什市从事强迫劳动。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区图木舒克市监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/13.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/13.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">艾山江·卡日（维）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1969</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，维吾尔族，维名<span lang="EN-US">Hesenjan Qari</span>，新疆克孜勒苏柯尔克孜自治州（简称“克州”）阿图什市松他克乡人，乌兹别克斯坦国移居者，纺织品对外贸易经销商，中国在押政治犯。早年曾生长于新疆西南部的克孜勒苏柯尔克孜自治州首府阿图什市，中学毕业后开始经商，并多年从事中国和中亚（主指乌兹别克斯坦国等）之间的纺织品贸易；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年，因在乌兹别克斯坦遇到其妻子古尔森（维族名<span lang="EN-US">Gulshan Manapova</span>，乌兹别克斯坦国公民，从小讲维吾尔语和俄语，其父母家人曾因中国文化大革命而被迫于<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年逃离中国前往哈萨克斯坦，后移居乌兹别克斯坦国而成为该国合法公民），遂结婚生子，并一起为自己的家庭及未来而努力经营、打造；自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年起，其在哈萨克开办了一家布料店，将新疆的纺织品拿到哈国买卖，生意十分兴隆，然当其在中国境内的家人电告要其回国探访，同时，新疆老家政府亦要求其尽快回国接受问讯之后，其人生轨迹骤然发生变化；起初回国，其及妻子儿女均未料到中共政府会对他感兴趣，但在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月返回新疆一周之后，其即被当地官员带走问讯，并将其护照和哈萨克居民卡没收；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又被送一所再教育营关押，从此失联；后知<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其曾被阿图什市法院以不具名罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，但同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，据在国内的亲戚说又被警方带回阿图什市第五区营地接受再教育，并警方要求其亲戚为他寄送衣服；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，其被阿图什市法院再次以“加入恐怖组织”和“利用极端主义破坏执法”罪名重新重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月；据悉，自其被刑拘羁押至一审判刑上诉以来，一直身体健康极差，警方通知其亲戚他已在医院接受治疗；因其被抓捕判刑，其妻子儿女一家人长期深陷生活窘境；其在再教育营培训期间，曾和众多人一起被强制灌输共产主义意识形态，教授中共强调的所谓中国文化，并拒绝沿袭和使用伊斯兰教习俗等等。目前在疆生产建设兵团第三师图木舒克监狱第五监区服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/146.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/146.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">艾则孜•艾买提（维吾尔）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">47</span>岁，新疆阿克苏地区维族教长。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月因皮山县一个村市集从事宗教教学活动，被当地公安局拘捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判入狱<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安然：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本名崔浩新、济南回民作家、诗人（即推友<span lang="EN-US">@ismaelan </span>）。安然现年<span lang="EN-US">41</span>岁的安然曾在官方刊物发表过自己的作品，其中有作品被收录到中国作家协会编选的“新时期少数民族文学选”。他早前发表的《我的诗歌志》，记录其诗歌生涯中有一大部分为关注新疆的内容。此前<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月曾因在推特转发和发布的有关新疆“再教育营”的报道和文字等言论遭警方抓捕，后都有惊无险获释。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日即农历春节除夕夜遭济南警方刑事拘留，罪名是寻衅滋事。目前音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">昂扎（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，原比如镇孟庆村干部，政治异议人士，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年以来，一直担任那曲地区比如镇孟庆村的村干部；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，因中共当局在其所在县各乡村展开‘爱国再教育运动’，并强迫藏民在各家屋顶上悬挂五星红旗，此举引起比如县农牧民、学生、僧人、尼姑、作家、歌手等各类人士的同声抗议，并发起连串示威活动，成为继<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年后在西藏自治区内最大的示威抗议活动，随引发中共当局的极度恐惧，将比如县视为极不稳定地区，曾先后集结大批军警实施“维稳”，肆意拘捕僧俗藏人，对当地有影响力的藏人处以重刑，并采取‘对内严厉打击示威民众，对外严密封锁消息’等严打措施；在此背景下，昂扎所在孟庆村的藏民亦因参与了公开抗议与示威活动，遂遭致当局的严酷打压，于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被当地警方以涉嫌“参与抗议示威”，“秘密组织相关人员在家里召开会议”等罪由刑拘，后被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被当地法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罪名不详。目前在西藏自治区一家监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">奥坎（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生不详，新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰地区人，哈萨克族，穆斯林，伊犁哈萨克自治州阿尔泰地区哈巴河县清真寺阿訇（即伊斯兰宗教事务主持人），伊斯兰知名宗教领袖，中国在押良心犯。近年来，因新疆地区局势日益紧张，中共当局加强了对新疆各民族在宗教信仰上的高压管控手段和措施，哈萨克族人也不例外；这期间，因奥坎是阿尔泰地区哈萨克族群中知名宗教界领袖，影响力大，遂当局严密监控，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年又因其按照本民族及宗教习俗为死者做了传统的祷告仪式，被当地警方偷拍，随后即以此问罪，被抓刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初，其被阿尔泰地区哈巴河县法院以不具名罪名秘判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前羁押或服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">B.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴依木拉提·那如孜别克（哈）、巴和提古丽·吾力拜依（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴给拉·吾力拜依（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白宝华、白国显、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">白兴文</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">白雪松、白亚娟</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白玉福、白玉珍、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">白玛益西（藏）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">柏淑琴</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">班阔吉（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">边雪梅、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">鲍桂琴、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">包国华、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">包万明</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卞丽潮、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卞丽训</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">别克什•马铁甫汗、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">别热克汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>朵兰汗（哈萨克）、别依力汗•萨合达提及其儿子（哈萨克）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、不列斯白克•叶尔买克巴依（哈）、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴依木拉提·那如孜别克（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1990</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族，伊宁县卡拉亚尕奇乡奥依曼布拉克村居民，曾任当地协警，哈萨克斯坦斯坦国绿卡持有者，中国在押政治犯。早期曾到上海市某高中上学；毕业后，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月又曾前往中国邻国——哈萨克斯坦共和国（又称哈萨克斯坦斯坦国，简称“哈国”），在阿拉木图市大学攻读学位，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月返回中国新疆；因其在哈国留学期间曾获取绿卡（即拥有哈国永久居住权），且留学期间在<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日等，曾在社交平台“百度贴吧”上多次发表中共政府视为的“民族敏感性”文章，回国生活数载后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，突然被新疆伊宁县警方莫名抓走，送当地政治教育中心接受“再教育培训”（实则被监禁羁押）；被囚长达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后，因其对培训方式及内容等心存抵触，培训结果表现不佳，故不仅未被释放返家，反被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被新疆伊宁县法院一审以“煽动民族仇恨罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。目前在新疆乌苏监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/10.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/10.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴和提古丽·吾力拜依：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1977</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市人，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US"> Baktgul Oralbaikizi</span>，穆斯林信徒，前伊犁哈萨克自治州《奎屯日报》记者，中国在押良心犯。 早年曾一直在新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯日报社任职当记者，后与其兄长及小妹先后前往哈萨克斯坦国创业；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，原西藏自治区党委书记陈全国调任新疆当一把手，因强化要加强对新疆地区的管控，要求工作及生活在海外的维吾尔族、哈萨克族等中国公民（含海外留学生）必须立刻返回中国生活，其随与众哈萨克族同胞纷纷返回新疆；回国后最初两年，除去其护照被地方当局没收、出国权利受限外，生活尚能平安顺利，直至<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其突遭伊犁州奎屯市警方莫名抓捕，并送一家政治再教育转化营羁押，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其家人从奎屯市警方处得知，其被伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，罪名不清，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2037</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月；据悉，其丈夫受牵连屡遭警方恐吓威胁，被要求与妻子尽早离婚，被其断然拒绝。目前在新疆新源监狱（新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州新源县，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">868813</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴给拉·吾力拜依：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，哈萨克族，<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市人，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US">Bagila Oralbaikizi</span>，穆斯林信徒，个体商户经营者、理发店老板，奎屯市公民，中国在押良心犯。曾在伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市经营一家理发店十余年，后与兄长及姐姐先后前往哈萨克斯坦国创业；<span lang="EN-US"> 2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，因原西藏自治区党委书记陈全国调任新疆当一把手，强化要加强对新疆地区的控制，遂要求凡去海外留学、工作及生活的维吾尔族、哈萨克族等中国公民必须尽快返回国内生活，故其随与其兄姊及众哈萨克族同胞纷纷返回新疆；回国之初，政府当局虽将其护照予以没收、出国权利受到限制，但日常生活尚属平安顺利，直至<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其及其兄姊均遭伊犁州奎屯市警方突然抓捕，并送当地某政治再教育转化营关押，自此失去联系；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其家人从奎屯市警方处获悉，其被伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，罪名不清，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月；据悉，其丈夫屡遭警方施压，被要求与其妻离婚，被其夫断然拒绝。目前在新疆生产建设兵团农七师奎屯监狱（新疆维吾尔自治区<span lang="EN-US">/</span>克拉玛依市<span lang="EN-US">/</span>克拉玛依区<span lang="EN-US">/</span>共青镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">834034</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白宝华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">内蒙古赤峰市元宝山区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁左右，农村妇女，没有收入，家庭以收破烂维持生活。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午十一点左右，赤峰市元宝山区元宝山镇派出所韩立民带领三个便衣去白宝华家骚扰，非法抄家，抢劫大法书籍、台历（<span lang="EN-US">500</span>本左右）、<span lang="EN-US">14000</span>元现金及很多个人物品，并把白宝华抓捕。其中这<span lang="EN-US">14000</span>元是白宝华用来给儿子治大腿血栓从亲戚朋友处借来的钱，都被抢去说成是用来做法轮功资料。随后，白宝华被送至元宝山区看守所关押。后白宝华被赤峰中级法院宣判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白国显：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。白国显被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">白兴文：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东东营市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已年近<span lang="EN-US">70</span>，家住山东省东营市河口区孤岛镇协作二村。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，白兴文和<span lang="EN-US">2</span>女儿季英萍在家中被海滨分局警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>天之后，白兴文因身体原因被所谓的“取保候审”回了家。白兴文的大女儿季英梅早年也修炼过法轮功自从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日季英梅被海滨分局警察抓捕之日起，不到<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月的时间，季英梅就经历了中共邪党从身体上、经济上、精神上的高压迫害，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日清晨含冤离世，年仅<span lang="EN-US">45</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，白兴文再被滨海市公安局警察抓捕，关押在滨海市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，东营区法院法官以视频开庭的方式对白兴文判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金两万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" lang="EN-US">19</span>日午后，居住在鞍山市铁西区民政局附近的史颜影，在鞍山市一所养老院工作期间被抓捕，并被关押到岫岩看守所。她家中电脑、打印机等私有物品被抄走。警方于次日抓捕了去她家的白雪松。白雪松、史颜影，被警察抓捕、关押构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后，<span 0pt;">黑龙江省绥化市北林区有<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日同时被绥化市北林区“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”及派出所警察抓捕，其中包括白亚娟。后获悉，白亚娟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被送往黑龙江省女子监狱<span
