mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白玉福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江大庆市被迫流离失所的法轮功学员。原大庆市石油管理局测井公司武保科科长；妻子张立新，原大庆石油管理局物业二公司乘风热力分公司职工。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，白玉福和张立新开始修炼法轮功，按真、善、忍标准做好人。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，白玉福、张立新夫妇多次被中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，白玉福、张立新夫妇在辽宁省阜新市彰武县被警方抓捕，后刑事拘留、批捕、起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被彰武县法院视频开庭。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日获悉，白玉福被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，张立新被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。白玉福刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">白玉珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河南省信阳市浉河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1941</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日法轮功学员白玉珍、靳玉玲被信阳市警察入室抓捕，后被构陷至信阳市潢川县检察院、法院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在看守所遭开庭。靳玉玲<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁；白玉珍老人<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁，进法庭时，身体走路都不稳。在开庭过程中，靳玉玲、白玉珍一直还被强制戴着手铐。靳玉玲被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；白玉珍被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。白玉珍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b>信息来源</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html</span></u></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">白玛益西（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年出生，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Pema Yeshi</span>，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新龙县人，甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）尼达村农民，藏族人权捍卫者。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，随于被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处死刑，缓期两年执行，后改判为无期徒刑。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">柏淑琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省承德市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，女。其于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被承德市公安局双桥分局政保大队警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，家属收到逮捕通知书，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，承德市双桥区法院对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458755.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458755.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">班阔吉（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，女，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县城关镇人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者、政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾在当地发生示威活动时，因政治诉求而两次遭到当局数月拘押，获释后一直处于被严密监控中。<span lang="EN-US"> 2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日突然再次被抓，自此失联，后得知她被指控涉嫌“组织阿坝民众举办达赖喇嘛尊者八十岁寿辰活动”而遭逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，据悉当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">边雪梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省衡阳市衡山县法轮功学员。家住湖南省衡阳市衡山县开云镇。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，边雪梅被衡山长江派出所颜永初恶意举报，遭一伙警察闯入家中绑架。警察抢走她家中所有修炼用的经书、其它各种私人物品以及四千多元人民币。边雪梅被关押到衡阳市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午，衡山县检察院、法院对边雪梅非法开庭，当庭没有结果。据悉，法官要边雪梅当庭认罪保证今后不再炼法轮功，否则要判刑。边雪梅，一直讲真相，表示，按真善忍做好人没有错。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，衡山县法院再次对边雪梅视频开庭，宣称对边雪梅判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，所谓理由不是法律条文，而是法轮功学员边雪梅“拒不认错”，“不配合”。此后，被非法关押在衡阳市第一看守所的边雪梅仍被看守所和法院人员逼写“保证书”。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">鲍桂琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，家住黑龙江省齐齐哈尔富拉尔基区。因为信仰法轮大法，曾经多次被抓捕、关押、劳教和判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午，鲍桂琴去一法轮功学员家拜访，被齐齐哈尔市红宝石派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月末被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。鲍桂琴被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱八监区，被“转化”迫害，遭监狱指使的犯人暴力殴打、酷刑折磨。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/19/456918.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/19/456918.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">包国华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">浙江金华圣爱堂牧师，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被金华市公安局婺城分局以涉嫌非法经营罪、聚众扰乱社会秩序罪、隐匿会计凭证罪、侵占罪四个罪名刑事拘留。被抓之前，包牧师曾拒绝金华市宗教局强制整改（实质是拆除）新教堂顶部的十字架。包国华牧师拒绝的理由是<span lang="EN-US">-----</span>新教堂的施工、规划手续齐全，不是违法建筑，不应当整改（拆除）。在被拘留后的第<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日金华日报、浙江卫视以“清廉牧师”的贪婪人生大篇幅报道包国华牧师及其妻子邢文香牧师的所谓犯罪事实。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，包国华牧师被金华市婺城区法院控告犯有“职务侵占罪”、“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”、“非法经营罪”以及“隐匿会计凭证、会计账簿、财务会计报告罪”等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>项罪名，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，并处没收财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">60</span>万元，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">包万明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江鸡西市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>出生。鸡西市法轮功学员周克铭在发放法轮功资料时，被人诬告。鸡西市公安局鸡冠区公安分局国保、永昌派出所、铁西派出所采取跟踪、监控手段，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日抓捕了包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被非法关押在鸡西市看守所<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。包万明、周克铭、滕淑丽，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日遭鸡东法院以视频的方式开庭，近日得知，包万明被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、罚金十万元；滕淑丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元；周克铭被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。包万明刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">卞丽潮：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，河北省人，原河北省唐山市开滦第十中学教师，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。曾因信仰和修炼法轮功，而遭到中共警方长期监控；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年初，因中共当局通过监控手段得知有法轮功学员从事光盘盒生意，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，统一部署，以“大案”“要案”为目标，在河北、辽宁、山东等十数个省份集结各地国保、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”派出所警员，按照监听查获的名单，野蛮逮捕了一百多名法轮功学员，卞丽潮亦因法轮功学员身份而被河北省唐山市警方刑拘；逮捕刑拘期间，多次遭遇严刑逼供，其妻女受到严厉威胁，其家被抄，且家中做生意用的流动资金（注：其被抓走时，家中约有十几万元现金，尚未来得及存入银行）竟被警方非法侵占，并以开假单据方式诱骗其妻签字，谎称是法轮功资金，以示为“证据”；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被河北省唐山市中级法院以“信仰、修炼法轮功邪教”为罪由重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。最初在河北省保定监狱服刑，因其不堪忍受狱中酷刑折磨（注：狱方每天会派<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个狱警带着<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个犯人对其进行轮番“包夹”监控、折磨），致其心脏病等病情严重恶化，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日起转到河北省石家庄第四监狱第八监区服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">卞丽训：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东青岛法轮功学员。山东省青岛市四方区人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，金永新、卞丽训夫妇被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日分别被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/19/445121.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/19/445121.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">别克什·马铁甫汗：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">哈萨克族，<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，新疆阿尔泰市人，阿尔泰市布尔津县奥伊玛克乡卡台村公民，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US">Bikesh Manapqan</span>，哈萨克族企业家，中国在押维权人士。自中共政府对新疆维吾尔自治区各少数族裔采取愈加严苛的管理以来，其所在阿尔泰市布尔津县成为新疆当局“扫黑除恶专项行动”的重灾区（之一），期间，其全家（含其父亲和两个兄长等）因在布尔津县喀纳斯湖风景区经办了一家知名的旅游公司，不仅为其家族赚得了较多收入，也为当地旅游业的发展提供了不小的便利，随被地方当局看重和欲加掠夺；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，阿尔泰地区布尔津县当局曾多次派人与其父等人谈判，试图以贿赂的方式让其放弃对喀纳斯湖风景区旅游公司的全部经营权，后被其拒绝，随遭记恨与迫害；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其被布尔津县奥伊玛克乡警方突然带走，直接送到当地一家“再教育营”关押，自此失联；后因其不愿接受“再教育营”对其的洗脑式培训，同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，遂与其父亲及两个哥哥被阿尔泰市布尔津县警方借“扫黑除恶”之名，以涉嫌“非法经营罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”等转为刑拘；后又被布尔津县检察院以涉嫌以同罪名正式批捕，指控其等数人因参与“暴力行为、敲诈勒索和霸凌行为、强征管理费、大肆打架、寻衅滋事、妨碍公务程序、参与喀纳斯旅游景区违法经营”等行为，触犯了国家的相关法律和规定，遂应予以逮捕、判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其一行多人“涉黑恶势力”案在阿尔泰市布尔津县法院统一开庭受审，其中，其被以“非法经营罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”等重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月；据悉，其家人之前一直无其更多讯息，直到<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，其妻子在一篇《扫黑除恶：布尔钦县首例公开汇编涉嫌“黑势力”案件》的官方文章中，才发现了其被判刑的具体信息。目前疑似在新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰市福海监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/7.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/7.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">别热克汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>朵兰汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州塔城地区额敏县人，塔城地区额敏县某清真寺主持，官派任命阿訇，良心犯。曾在清真寺主持工作<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，但仍因宗教信仰自由问题而被塔城地区额敏县警方于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年上半年拘捕，后被当局指控为：未经许可，以伊斯兰教传统方式给一对哈萨克族新婚人念尼卡，而这对婚夫妇在婚礼的第二天才正式登记领取结婚证，此举触犯了中共“其极端化”法令，于是很快被宣布逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被伊犁哈萨克自治州塔城地区法院以“从事非法宗教活动罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年。目前具体服刑地点不详，只知他被羁押在新疆昌吉州一所用来囚禁政治犯的大监狱中。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">别依力汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>萨合达提及其儿子：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆阿尔泰地区青河县阿热勒乡清真寺阿訇别依力汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>萨合达提，男，哈萨克族，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年春天被抓，至今无下落，。别依力汗的儿子，因在哈国官方宗教学校学过三个月的宗教知识，也被公安带走羁押。而别依力汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>萨合达提家族，在青河县属著名的宗教家族，他的父亲、爷爷都是阿訇，在当地有极高的知名度。由于百姓对其家族的尊敬，引来当局的恐惧，故遭迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">不列斯白克•叶尔买克巴依（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，新疆伊犁霍城县人，伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州霍城县生产建设兵团小麻扎<span lang="EN-US">61</span>团光明路<span lang="EN-US">084</span>号公民，哈萨克族，穆斯林，中国在押良心犯。被捕前，曾与家人海外旅游并暂留哈萨克斯坦共和国居住；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年返回中国后，不久即被伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州霍城县警方没收护照；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年前后，被以不明罪由（疑指对中共当局思想不忠等）抓捕，送入霍城县“教育培训中心”（又称“再教育营”）接受中共洗脑式教育，自此失联；后因在该“培训中心”拒绝认罪和配合接受再教育方式及其要求，遂被霍城县警方正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，被新疆伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州霍城县法院一审以不确罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年初。目前疑似在新疆伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州新源监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
</div>
